  - FastAPI (web framework)
  - NumPy, Pandas (data processing)
  - 100+ dependencies with complex C extensions

  Expected Duration:

  - First-time install: 5-15 minutes (depending on internet speed)
  - Subsequent installs: 2-5 minutes (packages cached)

  What's Taking Time:

  1. Large downloads: Some packages are 50-100+ MB
  2. Compiling C extensions: numpy, pandas, etc. compile native code
  3. Dependency resolution: pip has to figure out compatible versions

  Is It Stuck?

  Check if it's progressing:
  - Do you see new package names appearing?
  - Is the download speed showing (MB/s)?
  - Is disk activity happening?

  requirements.txt --verbose

     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ PHASE 0: AI GATEWAY DEPLOYMENT (CRITICAL PREREQUISITE)                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Guide 0: AI Gateway VM Setup & Deployment                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ File: .gemini-guides/00_ai_gateway_deployment.md                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Content Structure:                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Prerequisites                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - GCP account with billing enabled                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Docker installed locally (for building image)                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - SSH key pair generated                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Domain name for AI Gateway (optional but recommended)                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Part 1: Local Preparation                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Build Docker Image:                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Navigate to ai_service directory                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ cd ai_service/                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Build Docker image                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker build -t nexus-ai-gateway:latest .                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Test locally                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker run -d \                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --name ai-gateway-test \                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   -p 8000:8000 \                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --env-file .env \                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   nexus-ai-gateway:latest                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Verify                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ curl http://localhost:8000/health                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Expected: {"status": "ok"}                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Stop test container                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker stop ai-gateway-test                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker rm ai-gateway-test                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Push to Container Registry:                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Option A: GCP Artifact Registry                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud auth configure-docker us-central1-docker.pkg.dev                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker tag nexus-ai-gateway:latest \                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   us-central1-docker.pkg.dev/YOUR_PROJECT/nexus/ai-gateway:latest       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker push                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ us-central1-docker.pkg.dev/YOUR_PROJECT/nexus/ai-gateway:latest         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Option B: Docker Hub (simpler for MVP)                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker tag nexus-ai-gateway:latest                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker push YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Part 2: GCP VM Provisioning                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Create VM Instance:                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud compute instances create nexus-ai-gateway \                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --project=YOUR_PROJECT_ID \                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --zone=us-central1-a \                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --machine-type=e2-medium \                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --boot-disk-size=20GB \                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --boot-disk-type=pd-standard \                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --image-family=ubuntu-2204-lts \                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --image-project=ubuntu-os-cloud \                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --tags=http-server,https-server                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Firewall Rules:                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Allow HTTPS (443) from internet                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud compute firewall-rules create allow-https \                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --allow tcp:443 \                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --target-tags https-server \                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --description "Allow HTTPS traffic"                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Allow SSH (22) for management                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud compute firewall-rules create allow-ssh \                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --allow tcp:22 \                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --description "Allow SSH access"                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Reserve Static IP (Recommended):                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud compute addresses create nexus-ai-gateway-ip \                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --region=us-central1                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Assign to VM                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud compute instances add-access-config nexus-ai-gateway \           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --zone=us-central1-a \                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --access-config-name "External NAT" \                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --address $(gcloud compute addresses describe nexus-ai-gateway-ip     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --region=us-central1 --format='get(address)')                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Part 3: VM Configuration                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SSH into VM:                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ gcloud compute ssh nexus-ai-gateway --zone=us-central1-a                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Install Docker:                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Update packages                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo apt update                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo apt upgrade -y                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Install Docker                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com -o get-docker.sh                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo sh get-docker.sh                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Add user to docker group                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo usermod -aG docker $USER                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ newgrp docker                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Verify                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker --version                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Create Environment File:                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Create app directory                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ mkdir -p /home/$USER/nexus-ai                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ cd /home/$USER/nexus-ai                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Create .env file                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ nano .env                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Add these secrets:                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SUPABASE_URL=https://your-project.supabase.co                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY=your-service-role-key                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ GEMINI_API_KEY=your-gemini-api-key                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ PORT=8000                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Pull and Run Container:                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Pull from registry                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker pull YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Run with auto-restart                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker run -d \                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --name nexus-ai-gateway \                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --restart unless-stopped \                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   -p 8000:8000 \                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   --env-file .env \                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Check logs                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ docker logs -f nexus-ai-gateway                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Verify health                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ curl http://localhost:8000/health                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Part 4: Reverse Proxy Setup (Caddy)                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Install Caddy:                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo apt install -y debian-keyring debian-archive-keyring               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ apt-transport-https                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ curl -1sLf 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/caddy/stable/gpg.key' | sudoв”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ  gpg --dearmor -o /usr/share/keyrings/caddy-stable-archive-keyring.gpg  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ curl -1sLf 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/caddy/stable/debian.deb.txt'в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ  | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/caddy-stable.list                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo apt update                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo apt install caddy                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Configure Caddy:                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo nano /etc/caddy/Caddyfile                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Caddyfile content:                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ # Replace with your domain or use IP                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ai-gateway.yourdomain.com {                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     reverse_proxy localhost:8000                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     # Optional: Basic auth for admin endpoints                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     # basicauth /metrics/* {                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     #     admin $2a$14$...                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     # }                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ }                                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Reload Caddy:                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo systemctl reload caddy                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ sudo systemctl enable caddy  # Auto-start on boot                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Part 5: DNS Configuration (If Using Domain)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Point DNS to VM IP:                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Type: A Record                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Name: ai-gateway                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Value: [VM_STATIC_IP]                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ TTL: 3600                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Wait for propagation (5-10 minutes), then test:                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ curl https://ai-gateway.yourdomain.com/health                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Part 6: Vercel Integration                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Update Vercel Environment Variables:                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Variable: AI_GATEWAY_URL                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Value: https://ai-gateway.yourdomain.com                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Or use IP directly (less secure):                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ AI_GATEWAY_URL=https://[VM_STATIC_IP]                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Redeploy Vercel app to pick up new env var.                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ File: .gemini-guides/05_rfq_delta_gate.md                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Content Structure:                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ API Endpoint                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Complete Next.js API route code:                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // app/api/documents/[id]/hash-requirements/route.ts                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Extract requirements from document                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Generate SHA256 hash                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Compare with previous version                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Return detailed diff                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Logic Flow:                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Fetch document by ID                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Parse requirements section (AI-based extraction)                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Generate hash using crypto library                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Query previous version hash from document_versions table             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 5. If different, generate diff using diff library                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 6. Return structured response with changes highlighted                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ UI Component                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Complete React component:                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // components/documents/DeltaGateAlert.tsx                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Prominent banner at top of document view                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Side-by-side diff viewer                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - Change summary with impact labels                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // - "Acknowledge & Proceed" button workflow                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Integration Points:                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Hook into DocumentDetail.tsx view                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Check for delta on document load                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Store acknowledgment in document_acknowledgments table                в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ implementation status                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ EXECUTIVE SUMMARY                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Your ERP system now has two complementary monitoring layers working     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ together:                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Diagnostic Mesh (Infrastructure Health) - Ensures system is safe     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Intelligent Mesh (Business Logic AI) - Ensures business is healthy   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Both are complete and ready for integration into CI/CD and daily        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ operations.                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ PART 1: DIAGNOSTIC MESH (INFRASTRUCTURE HEALTH)                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ What It Does: Zero-tolerance failure detection for infrastructure       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ (endpoints, database, latency, RLS, schema)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Implementation Status: вң… Complete - Scripts created, ready to run      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Components Delivered                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Endpoint Registry (scripts/diagnostic/endpoint-registry.ts)          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Master catalog of 24+ API endpoints                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Each endpoint has a "health contract" with:                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Latency budgets (p50, p95, p99 milliseconds)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Error rate ceiling (e.g., 0.1%)                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Auth requirements (required/optional/none)                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - RLS enforcement flag                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Response schema validation                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Criticality level (BLOCKING/CRITICAL/HIGH/MEDIUM)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Example Entry:                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ {                                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   name: 'List Projects',                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   method: 'GET',                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   path: '/api/projects',                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   latency: { p50: 50, p95: 150, p99: 500 },                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   errorRate: 0.001,                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   authContext: 'required',                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   requiredRLS: true,                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   criticality: 'CRITICAL',                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ }                                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Health Probe Runner (scripts/diagnostic/run-health-probes.ts)        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Makes real HTTP requests to all endpoints (not mocks)                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Validates against contracts:                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Latency within budget?                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Status code correct?                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Auth enforced?                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… RLS blocking unauthorized access?                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Response schema matches?                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Generates JSON reports to ./reports/ directory                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Exit codes: 0=PASS, 1=DEGRADED, 2=FAIL                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Usage:                                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run diagnose                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Deployment Gate (scripts/diagnostic/deployment-gate.ts)              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Master pre-deployment enforcement gate                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Blocks unsafe deployments before they reach production                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Runs 8 critical checks:                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   a. вң… Endpoint Health (all probes pass)                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   b. вң… Build Succeeds (npm run build completes)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   c. вң… TypeScript Check (no compilation errors)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   d. вң… Environment Variables (all required vars set)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   e. вң… Schema Integrity (database tables exist)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   f. вң… Lint (code style passes)                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   g. вң… Build Output (artifacts present)                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   h. вң… Git Status (no uncommitted changes)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Exit codes: 0=PASS (deploy), 1=FAIL (block deployment)                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Usage:                                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run diagnose:gate                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Unified Health Check (scripts/health/unified-health-check.ts)        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Meta-command that combines all health checks                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Colorized terminal output with status icons                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Generates comprehensive report:                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Endpoint health summary                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - API health (/api/health endpoint)                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Build status                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Agent status                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Overall system score (0-100)                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Recommendations for fixes                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Supports JSON export for dashboards                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Usage:                                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run health              # Quick check                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run health:export       # Save JSON report                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Continuous Monitoring Architecture (24/7)                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Document Reference: .gemini-guides/CONTINUOUS_MONITORING_SYSTEM.md      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 6 Monitoring Layers:                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Endpoint Probes (Every 5 minutes)                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Vercel Cron or AWS Lambda                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Makes HTTP requests to all endpoints                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Stores results, triggers alerts on threshold violations             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Application Logging (Every request)                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - logger.ts logs every API call with latency, status, errors          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Exports to Sentry/Datadog                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Real-time metrics visible on dashboard                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Database Health Jobs (Hourly/Daily via pg_cron)                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - check_for_corruption() - Every 30 minutes                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - detect_schema_drift() - Daily 2 AM                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - validate_rls_coverage() - Daily 3 AM                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - process_escalations() - Hourly                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Alert Engine (Real-time)                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Compares metrics to thresholds                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Escalation matrix:                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ       - INFO вҶ’ Log only                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - WARNING вҶ’ Slack notification                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - CRITICAL вҶ’ Page L1 engineer                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - CATASTROPHIC вҶ’ Auto-rollback + page manager                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 5. Human Response (On-call engineers)                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - L1 Engineer: 15 min acknowledgment                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - L2 Manager: 5 min escalation                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - L3 VP: Immediate escalation                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 6. Autonomous Remediation (Self-healing)                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Auto-rollback on catastrophic failure                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Switch to read-only mode                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Disable write endpoints                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Verify recovery with re-probe                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Detection Speed: < 5 minutes                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Response Speed: < 15 minutes                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Coverage: 24/7, zero silent failures                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ PART 2: INTELLIGENT MESH (BUSINESS LOGIC AI)                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ What It Does: Autonomous AI agents that process documents, detect       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ compliance issues, answer questions, and enforce security               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Implementation Status: вң… Already in codebase - Fully operational       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ The 4 Agents                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Agent P1: Contract Extractor                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Role: Document processing automation                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Triggers: New document upload, manual extraction request              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Actions:                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Reads PDFs/contracts uploaded by users                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Extracts key fields: parties, dates, values, obligations,           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ deliverables                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Inserts structured data into documents table                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Logs extraction to agent_activity (immutable audit trail)           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Output: Structured metadata for downstream workflows                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Agent P5: Risk & Compliance Monitor                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Role: Proactive risk detection across portfolio                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Triggers: Daily scheduled scan, on-demand "GLOBAL_PORTFOLIO" scan     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Actions:                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Scans all projects for compliance gaps                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Detects missing safety documents                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Flags expired certifications                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Identifies policy violations                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Highlights stagnant projects (no updates > 7 days)                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Output: Creates alerts, updates risk heatmap, flags projects          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Integration: Powers "Execute Global Compliance Scan" in AgentConsole  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Agent P9: Knowledge Core                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Role: Semantic search and AI chat                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Triggers: Background document indexing, user chat queries             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Actions:                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Builds knowledge graph from all documents                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Enables natural language queries                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Powers ChatAssistant component ("Ask AI" feature)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Output: Contextual answers about projects, contracts, compliance      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Example Query: "How many projects are overdue?" вҶ’ Analyzes data вҶ’     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Returns specific projects with delay details                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Agent S1: Security Guard                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Role: Real-time access control enforcement                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Triggers: Continuous monitoring, suspicious activity detection        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Actions:                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Verifies RLS policies are applied correctly                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Detects privilege escalation attempts                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Enforces RBAC tier rules (L1-L4 permissions)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Blocks unauthorized access                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Output: Security event logs, access denials                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - Integration: Complements diagnostic mesh's RLS gap detection with     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ active enforcement                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Agent Infrastructure                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ File: utils/agent.ts                                                    в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ }                                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ в”Ӯ YOUR PRODUCTION SYSTEM                                      в”Ӯ         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ         в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җ P1 Agent: Extract contracts                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "Parse this tender spec вҶ’ structured data"                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җ P5 Agent: Detect compliance issues                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "Find stagnant projects, missing safety docs"                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җ P9 Agent: Answer questions                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "What's the budget for project XYZ?"                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ S1 Agent: Enforce access control                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ       в””в”Җ "Is this user allowed to view this?"                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ LAYER 3: Human Response                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ On-call engineer + AI agents collaborate                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ      в”ңв”Җ Diagnostic mesh: "Database down!"                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ      в”ңв”Җ Intelligent mesh: "All queries fail, likely migration lock"     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ      в””в”Җ Engineer fixes root cause                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Clear Division of Responsibilities:                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ        в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ 2. Test Health Commands                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run health              # See current system status                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run diagnose            # Test endpoint probes                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ npm run diagnose:gate       # Run pre-deployment checks                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Integrate into Workflow                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Add npm run diagnose:gate to CI/CD pipeline (before deployment)     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Schedule continuous probes (Vercel Cron or AWS Lambda)              в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ PART 7: CRITICAL SUCCESS METRICS                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Diagnostic Mesh Working When:                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… 100% of deployments pass the gate                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… All endpoints maintain latency budgets                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… 0 undetected schema drifts                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… 0 privilege escalations                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Alerts trigger within 5 minutes of threshold violation             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… On-call engineers acknowledge within 15 minutes                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Intelligent Mesh Working When:                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… P1 Agent extracts 95%+ of contracts correctly                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… P5 Agent detects compliance issues before human review             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… P9 Agent answers questions with 90%+ accuracy                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… S1 Agent blocks 100% of unauthorized access attempts               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… All agent actions logged to immutable audit trail                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Overall System Health:                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Infrastructure safe (Diagnostic Mesh: PASS)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Business healthy (Intelligent Mesh: Active)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Zero silent failures                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Detection < 5 min, Response < 15 min                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Complete observability across all layers                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ PART 8: COMMON QUESTIONS & ANSWERS                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: Do I need both meshes?                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Yes. Diagnostic ensures infrastructure is safe (endpoints, database, в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ latency). Intelligent ensures business is healthy (compliance,          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ contracts, risks). One without the other = incomplete observability.    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: How often do health checks run?                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Continuous probes (every 5 min), database jobs (hourly/daily),       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ deployment gate (pre-deployment only), unified health (on-demand).      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: What happens when a check fails?                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Depends on severity:                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - INFO вҶ’ Log only                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - WARNING вҶ’ Slack notification                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - CRITICAL вҶ’ Page L1 engineer (15 min SLA)                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - CATASTROPHIC вҶ’ Auto-rollback + page manager                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: Can agents trigger health checks?                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Not currently, but you can add this. Example: P5 Agent detects       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ stagnant project вҶ’ triggers diagnostic mesh to check if infrastructure  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ issue caused it.                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: How do I add a new endpoint?                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Add entry to endpoint-registry.ts with latency budget, auth          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ requirements, RLS flag. Run npm run diagnose to validate.               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: What if deployment gate blocks me?                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Fix the failing check first. Gate protects production from unsafe    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ code. Common failures: endpoint timeout, build error, missing env vars, в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ RLS gap.                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Q: Are the guides (1-8) still relevant?                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ A: Yes. Guides 1-3 (migrations, pg_cron, verification) are immediate.   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Guides 4-7 (resource management, delta gate, validation, performance)   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ are next phase. Guide 8 (production deployment) is final step.          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ SUMMARY FOR GEMINI                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ What You Have:                                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Complete diagnostic mesh (infrastructure health checks)            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Complete intelligent mesh (4 autonomous AI agents)                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Unified health command (npm run health)                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Deployment gate blocking unsafe deploys                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Comprehensive documentation (5 guides)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Clear architecture (dual-dashboard pattern)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ What You Need to Do:                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Test health commands locally                                         в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ   - Audience: Project managers                                          в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ   - Granular site performance                                           в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ   - Fields: RECORD_ID, ARTIFACT, STATUS, TIMESTAMP, LAST_MODIFIED       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Audience: Compliance officers, auditors                             в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Features                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ injection)                                                              в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ UI-integrated)                                                          в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ 5. Update Executive Cockpit architecture section                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 6. Document dashboard components inventory (all 23)                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 7. Add signals object specification                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 8. Update component organization tree                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Estimated Effort: 4-6 hours                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Option B: Refactor Implementation to Match Documentation                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Pros:                                                                   в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ DASHBOARD DESIGN ASSESSMENT: 2026 STANDARDS                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ User Requirement: "Extremely clean, slick, and most importantly 2026 in в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ style"                                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Current Status: Mixed - has modern elements but needs refinement        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ CURRENT DASHBOARD ANALYSIS                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ What's Working (2026-Aligned) вң…                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Glassmorphism & Depth                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Dark glass panels with backdrop blur                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Layered surfaces with subtle shadows                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Modern, on-trend                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Information Architecture                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Clear hierarchy: KPIs вҶ’ Projects вҶ’ Risk                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Signal-driven alerts at top                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Good prioritization                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Real-time Elements                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Live sync countdown (T-Minus timer)                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Pulsing indicators for critical items                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Dynamic, responsive                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Micro-interactions                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Hover effects with scale transforms                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Animated progress bars                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Fade-in transitions                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вң… Polished feel                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ What's Outdated (Not 2026) вқҢ                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Visual Overload                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - 23 components = too cluttered                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - "Cyberpunk/industrial" aesthetic feels 2022-2023                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Neon cyan/teal accents are dated                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ Not clean or minimal                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Layout Density                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Too much happening at once                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - No breathing room (gap-6 is tight)                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Information hierarchy unclear                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ Overwhelming, not slick                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Color Palette                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Heavy neon usage (cyan, emerald, rose)                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - High contrast everywhere                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ Feels aggressive, not sophisticated                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Typography                                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Uppercase tracking-widest everywhere                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Multiple font sizes without clear system                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ Lacks refinement                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 5. Missing 2026 Patterns                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ No AI copilot integration                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ No natural language interface                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ No adaptive/contextual layout                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ No ambient animations                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - вқҢ No spatial design (depth layers)                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2026 DESIGN STANDARDS                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Based on current trends (Apple Vision Pro, Linear, Vercel, Arc Browser, в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Notion AI):                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Core Principles                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Calm Technology                                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Information appears when needed                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Ambient awareness, not constant alerts                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Subtle gradients, not neon                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Spatial Design                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - True depth with parallax                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Frosted glass with depth blur                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Floating elements                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Z-axis layering                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. AI-Native                                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Copilot always accessible                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Contextual suggestions                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Natural language queries                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Predictive UI                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Minimal Maximalism                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Dense information, clean presentation                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - White space is intentional                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Typography does heavy lifting                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Color used sparingly                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 5. Motion Design                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Purposeful animations                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Elastic easing (not linear)                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - State transitions feel physical                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Hover states are subtle                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ RECOMMENDATIONS: 2026 DASHBOARD REDESIGN                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Option A: Evolution (Keep Structure, Refine Aesthetics) рҹҺЁ              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Effort: 2-3 weeks                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Risk: Low                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Changes:                                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 1. Color Palette Refinement                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /* Replace neon with sophisticated neutrals */                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --primary: #f5f5f7;      /* Near-white (Apple-grade) */                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --secondary: #1d1d1f;    /* Deep charcoal */                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --accent: #0071e3;       /* Subtle blue (not neon) */                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --success: #30d158;      /* Modern green */                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --warning: #ff9f0a;      /* Warm amber */                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --critical: #ff453a;     /* Refined red */                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /* Glassmorphism */                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --glass: rgba(29, 29, 31, 0.72);                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --glass-border: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08);                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. Typography System                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /* SF Pro Display / Inter Variable */                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --font-display: 'SF Pro Display', system-ui;                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --font-body: 'Inter Variable', system-ui;                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /* Hierarchy */                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --text-hero: 48px / 1.1 / 600;                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --text-title: 24px / 1.2 / 600;                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --text-body: 16px / 1.5 / 400;                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --text-caption: 13px / 1.4 / 400;                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /* Remove ALL-CAPS tracking-widest */                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 3. Spacing System                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /* More generous breathing room */                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --space-xs: 8px;                                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --space-sm: 16px;                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --space-md: 24px;   /* Default gap */                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --space-lg: 48px;                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ --space-xl: 96px;                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 4. Component Consolidation                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Reduce 23 вҶ’ 12 components                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Merge duplicates:                                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ       - RiskHeatmap + RiskHeatmapV2 вҶ’ Single version                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - TenderList + TendersDueSoonPanel вҶ’ Unified                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Archive deprecated: NotificationsPanel, SystemStatusConsole         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 5. Layout Simplification                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Remove Signal Cards at top (too noisy)                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Make KPI band cleaner (larger numbers, less decoration)             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Reduce right sticky panel width (400px вҶ’ 320px)                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Add more white space between sections                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Result: Cleaner, more sophisticated, still recognizable                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Option B: Revolution (Clean Slate, 2026-First) рҹҡҖ                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Effort: 6-8 weeks                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Risk: High                                                              в”Ӯ

     в”Ӯ 1. вң… Clerk Middleware Fixed (middleware.ts)                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Previous Issue: Middleware was bypassed completely, causing auth        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ warnings.                                                               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Solution Applied:                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // Conditional middleware based on env var                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ const clerkEnabled =                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Boolean((process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY ?? '').trim());  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ const middleware = clerkEnabled                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   ? clerkMiddleware(async (auth, req) => {                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ       if (!isPublicRoute(req)) {                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ         await auth.protect();                                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ       }                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     })                                                                  в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   : () => NextResponse.next();                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Impact:                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Proper Clerk authentication when enabled                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Graceful fallback when disabled (demo mode)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Public routes for AI health endpoints: /api/ai/ready,              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ /api/ai/health, /api/ai/version                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Resolves auth() warnings from earlier diagnostic runs              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Status: PRODUCTION-READY вң…                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ ---                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ 2. вң… RAG Bulk Ingestion Disabled (app/api/rag/ingest-all/route.ts)     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Previous Issue: Bulk ingestion could timeout on Vercel (5-minute limit).в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Solution Applied:                                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ // Returns 410 (Gone) status                                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ return NextResponse.json({                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   outcome: 'failed',                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   error: {                                                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     code: 'LEGACY_ENDPOINT_DISABLED',                                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     message: 'Bulk RAG ingestion is disabled on Vercel. Use the externalв”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ  AI Gateway indexing API/worker.'                                       в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   }                                                                     в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ }, { status: 410 });                                                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ Impact:                                                                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Prevents timeout errors in production                              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Clear error message directs users to external worker               в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Vercel-optimized architecture                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ - вң… Individual ingestion still works via /api/rag/ingest               в”Ӯ

     ARCHITECTURAL CLARIFICATION: DASHBOARD vs EXECUTIVE COCKPIT

     Date: 2026-01-29
     Purpose: Clarify whether to keep or remove the Executive Cockpit module
     Question: User asked if Executive Cockpit should be removed (potential
     redundancy with Dashboard)

     RECOMMENDATION: KEEP BOTH вң…

     After thorough codebase analysis, both modules serve distinct purposes 
     and should be retained.

     ---
     ANALYSIS SUMMARY

     Main Dashboard (Operations Command Center)

     Target Users: Project managers, operations team, daily users
     Purpose: Operational command center for active task execution
     Components:
     - 23 dashboard widgets (collapsible, expandable)
     - Real-time signal alerts (Global Intelligence Layer)
     - Document workflow management
     - Deadline tracking
     - Liability tracker
     - Tender management interface
     - Unified risk command panel (sticky right)
     - High information density for rapid decision-making

     Access: All users

     Executive Cockpit (Strategic Overview)

     Target Users: C-suite executives, board members, senior leadership
     Purpose: High-level strategic overview for leadership presentations
     Components:
     - 4 governance-grade metric blocks
     - Portfolio velocity charts (7D/30D financial trends)
     - Strategic volume visualization
     - Operational ledger (simplified project table)
     - Risk heatmap v2
     - Tab-based navigation (OVERVIEW / LEDGER / RISK)
     - Governance design system (minimalist, "Apple-grade")

     Access: L3+ tier only (restricted)

     Key Differences

     ---
     PHASE 0: AI GATEWAY DEPLOYMENT (CRITICAL PREREQUISITE)

     Guide 0: AI Gateway VM Setup & Deployment

     File: .gemini-guides/00_ai_gateway_deployment.md

     Content Structure:

     Prerequisites

     - GCP account with billing enabled
     - Docker installed locally (for building image)
     - SSH key pair generated
     - Domain name for AI Gateway (optional but recommended)

     Part 1: Local Preparation

     Build Docker Image:
     # Navigate to ai_service directory
     cd ai_service/

     # Build Docker image
     docker build -t nexus-ai-gateway:latest .

     # Test locally
     docker run -d \
       --name ai-gateway-test \
       -p 8000:8000 \
       --env-file .env \
       nexus-ai-gateway:latest

     # Verify
     curl http://localhost:8000/health
     # Expected: {"status": "ok"}

     # Stop test container
     docker stop ai-gateway-test
     docker rm ai-gateway-test

     Push to Container Registry:
     # Option A: GCP Artifact Registry
     gcloud auth configure-docker us-central1-docker.pkg.dev

     docker tag nexus-ai-gateway:latest \
       us-central1-docker.pkg.dev/YOUR_PROJECT/nexus/ai-gateway:latest

     docker push
     us-central1-docker.pkg.dev/YOUR_PROJECT/nexus/ai-gateway:latest

     # Option B: Docker Hub (simpler for MVP)
     docker tag nexus-ai-gateway:latest
     YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest
     docker push YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest

     Part 2: GCP VM Provisioning

     Create VM Instance:
     gcloud compute instances create nexus-ai-gateway \
       --project=YOUR_PROJECT_ID \
       --zone=us-central1-a \
       --machine-type=e2-medium \
       --boot-disk-size=20GB \
       --boot-disk-type=pd-standard \
       --image-family=ubuntu-2204-lts \
       --image-project=ubuntu-os-cloud \
       --tags=http-server,https-server

     Firewall Rules:
     # Allow HTTPS (443) from internet
     gcloud compute firewall-rules create allow-https \
       --allow tcp:443 \
       --target-tags https-server \
       --description "Allow HTTPS traffic"

     # Allow SSH (22) for management
     gcloud compute firewall-rules create allow-ssh \
       --allow tcp:22 \
       --description "Allow SSH access"

     Reserve Static IP (Recommended):
     gcloud compute addresses create nexus-ai-gateway-ip \
       --region=us-central1

     # Assign to VM
     gcloud compute instances add-access-config nexus-ai-gateway \
       --zone=us-central1-a \
       --access-config-name "External NAT" \
       --address $(gcloud compute addresses describe nexus-ai-gateway-ip
     --region=us-central1 --format='get(address)')

     Part 3: VM Configuration

     SSH into VM:
     gcloud compute ssh nexus-ai-gateway --zone=us-central1-a

     Install Docker:
     # Update packages
     sudo apt update
     sudo apt upgrade -y

     # Install Docker
     curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com -o get-docker.sh
     sudo sh get-docker.sh

     # Add user to docker group
     sudo usermod -aG docker $USER
     newgrp docker

     # Verify
     docker --version

     Create Environment File:
     # Create app directory
     mkdir -p /home/$USER/nexus-ai
     cd /home/$USER/nexus-ai

     # Create .env file
     nano .env

     Add these secrets:
     SUPABASE_URL=https://your-project.supabase.co
     SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY=your-service-role-key
     GEMINI_API_KEY=your-gemini-api-key
     PORT=8000

     Pull and Run Container:
     # Pull from registry
     docker pull YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest

     # Run with auto-restart
     docker run -d \
       --name nexus-ai-gateway \
       --restart unless-stopped \
       -p 8000:8000 \
       --env-file .env \
       YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest

     # Check logs
     docker logs -f nexus-ai-gateway

     # Verify health
     curl http://localhost:8000/health

     Part 4: Reverse Proxy Setup (Caddy)

     Install Caddy:
     sudo apt install -y debian-keyring debian-archive-keyring
     apt-transport-https
     curl -1sLf 'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/caddy/stable/gpg.key' |
     sudo gpg --dearmor -o 
     /usr/share/keyrings/caddy-stable-archive-keyring.gpg
     curl -1sLf 
     'https://dl.cloudsmith.io/public/caddy/stable/debian.deb.txt' | sudo
     tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/caddy-stable.list
     sudo apt update
     sudo apt install caddy

     Configure Caddy:
     sudo nano /etc/caddy/Caddyfile

     Caddyfile content:
     # Replace with your domain or use IP
     ai-gateway.yourdomain.com {
         reverse_proxy localhost:8000

         # Optional: Basic auth for admin endpoints
         # basicauth /metrics/* {
         #     admin $2a$14$...
         # }
     }

     Reload Caddy:
     sudo systemctl reload caddy
     sudo systemctl enable caddy  # Auto-start on boot

     Part 5: DNS Configuration (If Using Domain)

     Point DNS to VM IP:
     Type: A Record
     Name: ai-gateway
     Value: [VM_STATIC_IP]
     TTL: 3600

     Wait for propagation (5-10 minutes), then test:
     curl https://ai-gateway.yourdomain.com/health

     Part 6: Vercel Integration

     Update Vercel Environment Variables:
     Variable: AI_GATEWAY_URL
     Value: https://ai-gateway.yourdomain.com

     Or use IP directly (less secure):
     AI_GATEWAY_URL=https://[VM_STATIC_IP]

     Redeploy Vercel app to pick up new env var.

     Part 7: Verification

     Test from Vercel:
     # From your local machine
     curl https://your-vercel-app.vercel.app/api/ai/ready

     # Expected response:
     {
       "status": "online",
       "gateway_health": "ok",
       "timestamp": "2026-01-29T..."
     }

     Test agent functionality:
     1. Open AgentConsole in UI
     2. Check for "NEURAL LINK: SECURE" status
     3. Click "Execute Global Compliance Scan"
     4. Verify agent activity appears in IMMUTABLE_LEDGER

     Test ChatAssistant:
     1. Open chat widget in UI
     2. Send test message: "How many active projects?"
     3. Verify AI response appears

     Part 8: Monitoring & Maintenance

     View Container Logs:
     docker logs -f nexus-ai-gateway --tail 100

     Restart Container:
     docker restart nexus-ai-gateway

     Update Container (Zero Downtime):
     # Pull new image
     docker pull YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest

     # Stop old container
     docker stop nexus-ai-gateway
     docker rm nexus-ai-gateway

     # Run new version
     docker run -d \
       --name nexus-ai-gateway \
       --restart unless-stopped \
       -p 8000:8000 \
       --env-file .env \
       YOUR_DOCKERHUB_USER/nexus-ai-gateway:latest

     Set up automated health checks (cron):
     crontab -e

     # Add this line (check every 5 min)
     */5 * * * * curl -f http://localhost:8000/health || docker restart
     nexus-ai-gateway

     Success Criteria

     - вң… VM accessible via SSH
     - вң… Docker container running (docker ps shows nexus-ai-gateway)
     - вң… Health endpoint responds: curl http://localhost:8000/health
     - вң… HTTPS works: curl https://ai-gateway.yourdomain.com/health
     - вң… Vercel can reach gateway: /api/ai/ready returns "online"
     - вң… Agents show "NEURAL LINK: SECURE" in UI
     - вң… ChatAssistant responds to queries
     - вң… AgentConsole logs activity

     Troubleshooting

     Issue: Container won't start
     # Check logs
     docker logs nexus-ai-gateway

     # Common fixes:
     # - Verify .env file has all required secrets
     # - Check port 8000 isn't already in use: sudo lsof -i :8000
     # - Verify image pulled correctly: docker images

     Issue: Can't reach from Vercel
     # Check firewall
     sudo ufw status  # Should allow 443

     # Verify Caddy is running
     sudo systemctl status caddy

     # Test locally on VM first
     curl http://localhost:8000/health
     curl https://ai-gateway.yourdomain.com/health

     Issue: Agents still offline after deployment
     # Verify AI_GATEWAY_URL is set in Vercel
     # Check Vercel deployment logs
     # Test proxy endpoint directly:
     curl https://your-vercel-app.vercel.app/api/ai/health

     Estimated Time

     - VM Provisioning: 10 minutes
     - Docker Setup: 15 minutes
     - Caddy Configuration: 10 minutes
     - DNS Propagation: 5-10 minutes
     - Testing & Verification: 15 minutes
     - Total: ~1 hour

     PHASE 2: DEVELOPMENT GUIDES (Tasks #4-7)

     Guide 4: Resource Management System

     File: .gemini-guides/04_resource_management.md

     Database Schema

     Tables to Create:
     -- team_members: Employee/contractor records

     availability_end

     -- Columns: id, team_member_id, project_id, allocation_percentage,

     calculated_at

     3. AllocationPanel.tsx - Drag-drop assignment
     4. UtilizationChart.tsx - Recharts heatmap
     5. ManpowerImporter.tsx - CSV parser with Papa Parse

     Step-by-Step Implementation Order

     1. Create migration file вҶ’ Run in Supabase
     2. Create TypeScript types in types.ts
     3. Create data hooks in hooks/useResourceData.ts
     4. Build components in order (Grid вҶ’ Panel вҶ’ Chart вҶ’ Importer вҶ’ Page)

     6. Test with sample data

     Guide 5: RFQ Delta Gate

     File: .gemini-guides/05_rfq_delta_gate.md

     Content Structure:

     API Endpoint

     Complete Next.js API route code:
     // app/api/documents/[id]/hash-requirements/route.ts
     // - Extract requirements from document
     // - Generate SHA256 hash
     // - Compare with previous version
     // - Return detailed diff

     Logic Flow:
     1. Fetch document by ID
     2. Parse requirements section (AI-based extraction)
     3. Generate hash using crypto library
     4. Query previous version hash from document_versions table
     5. If different, generate diff using diff library
     6. Return structured response with changes highlighted

     UI Component

     Complete React component:
     // components/documents/DeltaGateAlert.tsx
     // - Prominent banner at top of document view
     // - Side-by-side diff viewer
     // - Change summary with impact labels
     // - "Acknowledge & Proceed" button workflow

     Integration Points:
     - Hook into DocumentDetail.tsx view
     - Check for delta on document load
     - Store acknowledgment in document_acknowledgments table

     Guide 6: Validation Framework

     File: .gemini-guides/06_validation_framework.md

     Complete TypeScript script:
     // scripts/validate-schema-drift.ts
     // - Connect to Supabase
     // - Query information_schema
     // - Compare against source of truth (consolidated schema)
     // - Generate drift report
