     ---
     GEMINI BRIEFING: DIAGNOSTIC & INTELLIGENT MESH ARCHITECTURE

     Date: 2026-01-29
     Status: Implementation Complete + Documentation Ready
     Purpose: Comprehensive briefing for Gemini on system architecture and
     implementation status

     ---
     EXECUTIVE SUMMARY

     Your ERP system now has two complementary monitoring layers working
     together:

     1. Diagnostic Mesh (Infrastructure Health) - Ensures system is safe
     2. Intelligent Mesh (Business Logic AI) - Ensures business is healthy

     Both are complete and ready for integration into CI/CD and daily
     operations.

     ---
     PART 1: DIAGNOSTIC MESH (INFRASTRUCTURE HEALTH)

     What It Does: Zero-tolerance failure detection for infrastructure
     (endpoints, database, latency, RLS, schema)

     Implementation Status: вң… Complete - Scripts created, ready to run

     Components Delivered

     1. Endpoint Registry (scripts/diagnostic/endpoint-registry.ts)

     - Master catalog of 24+ API endpoints
     - Each endpoint has a "health contract" with:
       - Latency budgets (p50, p95, p99 milliseconds)
       - Error rate ceiling (e.g., 0.1%)
       - Auth requirements (required/optional/none)
       - RLS enforcement flag
       - Response schema validation
       - Criticality level (BLOCKING/CRITICAL/HIGH/MEDIUM)

     Example Entry:
     {
       name: 'List Projects',
       method: 'GET',
       path: '/api/projects',
       latency: { p50: 50, p95: 150, p99: 500 },
       errorRate: 0.001,
       authContext: 'required',
       requiredRLS: true,
       criticality: 'CRITICAL',
     }

     2. Health Probe Runner (scripts/diagnostic/run-health-probes.ts)

     - Makes real HTTP requests to all endpoints (not mocks)
     - Validates against contracts:
       - вң… Latency within budget?
       - вң… Status code correct?
       - вң… Auth enforced?
       - вң… RLS blocking unauthorized access?
       - вң… Response schema matches?
     - Generates JSON reports to ./reports/ directory
     - Exit codes: 0=PASS, 1=DEGRADED, 2=FAIL

     Usage:
     npm run diagnose

     3. Deployment Gate (scripts/diagnostic/deployment-gate.ts)

     - Master pre-deployment enforcement gate
     - Blocks unsafe deployments before they reach production
     - Runs 8 critical checks:
       a. вң… Endpoint Health (all probes pass)
       b. вң… Build Succeeds (npm run build completes)
       c. вң… TypeScript Check (no compilation errors)
       d. вң… Environment Variables (all required vars set)
       e. вң… Schema Integrity (database tables exist)
       f. вң… Lint (code style passes)
       g. вң… Build Output (artifacts present)
       h. вң… Git Status (no uncommitted changes)
     - Exit codes: 0=PASS (deploy), 1=FAIL (block deployment)

     Usage:
     npm run diagnose:gate

     4. Unified Health Check (scripts/health/unified-health-check.ts)

     - Meta-command that combines all health checks
     - Colorized terminal output with status icons
     - Generates comprehensive report:
       - Endpoint health summary
       - API health (/api/health endpoint)
       - Build status
       - Agent status
       - Overall system score (0-100)
       - Recommendations for fixes
     - Supports JSON export for dashboards

     Usage:
     npm run health              # Quick check
     npm run health:export       # Save JSON report

     Continuous Monitoring Architecture (24/7)

     Document Reference: .gemini-guides/CONTINUOUS_MONITORING_SYSTEM.md

     6 Monitoring Layers:

     1. Endpoint Probes (Every 5 minutes)
       - Vercel Cron or AWS Lambda
       - Makes HTTP requests to all endpoints
       - Stores results, triggers alerts on threshold violations
     2. Application Logging (Every request)
       - logger.ts logs every API call with latency, status, errors
       - Exports to Sentry/Datadog
       - Real-time metrics visible on dashboard
     3. Database Health Jobs (Hourly/Daily via pg_cron)
       - check_for_corruption() - Every 30 minutes
       - detect_schema_drift() - Daily 2 AM
       - validate_rls_coverage() - Daily 3 AM
       - process_escalations() - Hourly
     4. Alert Engine (Real-time)
       - Compares metrics to thresholds
       - Escalation matrix:
           - INFO вҶ’ Log only
         - WARNING вҶ’ Slack notification
         - CRITICAL вҶ’ Page L1 engineer
         - CATASTROPHIC вҶ’ Auto-rollback + page manager
     5. Human Response (On-call engineers)
       - L1 Engineer: 15 min acknowledgment
       - L2 Manager: 5 min escalation
       - L3 VP: Immediate escalation
     6. Autonomous Remediation (Self-healing)
       - Auto-rollback on catastrophic failure
       - Switch to read-only mode
       - Disable write endpoints
       - Verify recovery with re-probe

     Detection Speed: < 5 minutes
     Response Speed: < 15 minutes
     Coverage: 24/7, zero silent failures

     ---
     PART 2: INTELLIGENT MESH (BUSINESS LOGIC AI)

     What It Does: Autonomous AI agents that process documents, detect 
     compliance issues, answer questions, and enforce security

     Implementation Status: вң… Already in codebase - Fully operational

     The 4 Agents

     Agent P1: Contract Extractor

     - Role: Document processing automation
     - Triggers: New document upload, manual extraction request
     - Actions:
       - Reads PDFs/contracts uploaded by users
       - Extracts key fields: parties, dates, values, obligations,
     deliverables
       - Inserts structured data into documents table
       - Logs extraction to agent_activity (immutable audit trail)
     - Output: Structured metadata for downstream workflows

     Agent P5: Risk & Compliance Monitor

     - Role: Proactive risk detection across portfolio
     - Triggers: Daily scheduled scan, on-demand "GLOBAL_PORTFOLIO" scan
     - Actions:
       - Scans all projects for compliance gaps
       - Detects missing safety documents
       - Flags expired certifications
       - Identifies policy violations
       - Highlights stagnant projects (no updates > 7 days)
     - Output: Creates alerts, updates risk heatmap, flags projects
     - Integration: Powers "Execute Global Compliance Scan" in AgentConsole

     Agent P9: Knowledge Core

     - Role: Semantic search and AI chat
     - Triggers: Background document indexing, user chat queries
     - Actions:
       - Builds knowledge graph from all documents
       - Enables natural language queries
       - Powers ChatAssistant component ("Ask AI" feature)
     - Output: Contextual answers about projects, contracts, compliance
     - Example Query: "How many projects are overdue?" вҶ’ Analyzes data вҶ’
     Returns specific projects with delay details

     Agent S1: Security Guard

     - Role: Real-time access control enforcement
     - Triggers: Continuous monitoring, suspicious activity detection
     - Actions:
       - Verifies RLS policies are applied correctly
       - Detects privilege escalation attempts
       - Enforces RBAC tier rules (L1-L4 permissions)
       - Blocks unauthorized access
     - Output: Security event logs, access denials
     - Integration: Complements diagnostic mesh's RLS gap detection with
     active enforcement

     Agent Infrastructure

     File: utils/agent.ts
     Console: components/pages/AgentConsole.tsx

     Audit Trail:
     Every agent action logged to agent_activity table:
     {
       agent_id: "P1",
       action_type: "POST" | "PATCH",
       document_id: "doc_12345",
       payload: { extraction_result: {...} },
       status: "completed" | "failed",
       hil_required: boolean,  // Human-in-loop flag
       timestamp: "2026-01-29T15:30:00Z"
     }

     AgentConsole Dashboard:
     - Shows 4 agents with load percentages and status
     - "Execute Global Compliance Scan" button (triggers P5)
     - Neural Link status indicator
     - 3 tabs: NEURAL_MESH, INTELLIGENCE_STREAM, IMMUTABLE_LEDGER

     PART 3: HOW THEY WORK TOGETHER

     The Complete Picture:

     в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

       в”ңв”Җ Endpoint Probes (every 5 min)
       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "Are endpoints alive? Latency OK? Auth working?"
       в”ңв”Җ Database Health Jobs (every 30 min - daily)
       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "Schema intact? RLS gaps? Data corruption?"
       в””в”Җ Alert Engine (real-time)
           в””в”Җ "Threshold exceeded? Page engineer?"

       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "Parse this tender spec вҶ’ structured data"

       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "Find stagnant projects, missing safety docs"
       в”ңв”Җ P9 Agent: Answer questions
       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җ "What's the budget for project XYZ?"
       в””в”Җ S1 Agent: Enforce access control
           в””в”Җ "Is this user allowed to view this?"

     LAYER 3: Human Response
       в””в”Җ On-call engineer + AI agents collaborate
          в”ңв”Җ Diagnostic mesh: "Database down!"
          в”ңв”Җ Intelligent mesh: "All queries fail, likely migration lock"
          в””в”Җ Engineer fixes root cause

     PART 4: DUAL-DASHBOARD PATTERN (CONSENSUS)

     Decision: KEEP BOTH вң…

     Main Dashboard (Operations Hub)

     - Users: Project managers, operations team, daily users
     - Purpose: Operational command center for task execution
     - Design: Dense, detailed, 23 widgets
     - Usage: Daily/hourly

     Executive Cockpit (Leadership Overview)

     - Users: C-suite executives, board members, L3+ tier
     - Purpose: Strategic overview for leadership presentations
     - Design: Minimalist, "Apple-grade", 4 metric blocks
     - Usage: Weekly/monthly

     This is deliberate, not duplication. Enterprise SaaS (Salesforce, Jira)
      uses this pattern.

     Optimization Opportunities:
     1. Extract shared KPI logic into reusable hook
     2. Unify risk visualization components
     3. Add cross-navigation buttons
     4. Document pattern in CLAUDE.md

     ---
     PART 8: COMMON QUESTIONS & ANSWERS

     Q: Do I need both meshes?
     A: Yes. Diagnostic ensures infrastructure is safe (endpoints, database,
      latency). Intelligent ensures business is healthy (compliance,
     contracts, risks). One without the other = incomplete observability.

     Q: How often do health checks run?
     A: Continuous probes (every 5 min), database jobs (hourly/daily),
     deployment gate (pre-deployment only), unified health (on-demand).

     Q: What happens when a check fails?
     A: Depends on severity:
     - INFO вҶ’ Log only
     - WARNING вҶ’ Slack notification
     - CRITICAL вҶ’ Page L1 engineer (15 min SLA)
     - CATASTROPHIC вҶ’ Auto-rollback + page manager

     Q: Can agents trigger health checks?
     A: Not currently, but you can add this. Example: P5 Agent detects 
     stagnant project вҶ’ triggers diagnostic mesh to check if infrastructure
     issue caused it.

     Q: How do I add a new endpoint?
     A: Add entry to endpoint-registry.ts with latency budget, auth 
     requirements, RLS flag. Run npm run diagnose to validate.

     Q: What if deployment gate blocks me?
     A: Fix the failing check first. Gate protects production from unsafe
     code. Common failures: endpoint timeout, build error, missing env vars,
      RLS gap.

     Q: Are the guides (1-8) still relevant?
     A: Yes. Guides 1-3 (migrations, pg_cron, verification) are immediate. 
     Guides 4-7 (resource management, delta gate, validation, performance)
     are next phase. Guide 8 (production deployment) is final step.

     Widget State Management

     Hook: useWidgetLayoutState.ts
     - Manages expand/collapse for all widgets
     - Accordion behavior (one expanded per group)
     - Persistent state via localStorage
     - Widget IDs: kpi_band, project_portfolio, tender_tracker,
     risk_command, deadlines, liability_tracker
     - Pinned widgets: risk_command, deadlines (can't be hidden)

     Data Flow

     Primary Hook: useDashboardData.ts
     - Real-time Supabase subscriptions on 6 tables
     - Returns: kpis, projects, tenders, documents, alerts, signals, 
     statusData, tasks, purchaseOrders
     - Signals object includes:
       - hasBacklog: Documents pending review > 10
       - stagnantProjects: No updates > 7 days
       - complianceIssues: Missing compliance scans
       - systemStatus: "Optimal" or "Congested"
       - riskDistribution: Critical/high/nominal/stable breakdown
       - poBreaches: Purchase order violations

     Supporting Hook: useDashboardLogic.ts
     - Extracts business logic from UI
     - Provides: activeTab, filteredProjects, deadlineTasks, liabilities, 
     riskAlerts

     ---
     REPORTS SYSTEM (100% UNDOCUMENTED)

     Architecture Overview

     Main File: ReportsPage.tsx (249 lines)
     Data Hook: useReports.ts (135 lines)
     Export Utils: reportGenerator.ts (505 lines), exportUtils.ts (48 lines)

     4 Report Profiles

     1. Executive Summary
       - High-level operational health
       - Fields: IDENTIFIER, VALUE_AED, STATUS, PROGRESS, RISK_VECTOR
       - Audience: C-suite, board members
     2. Standard Breakdown
       - Monthly project milestones
       - Fields: NAME, CODE, CLIENT, STATUS, LOCATION, PLATFORM
       - Audience: Project managers
     3. Depth Analysis
       - Granular site performance
       - Fields: All raw database fields
       - Audience: Technical teams, engineers
     4. Compliance Audit
       - Full traceability log with hierarchical drill-down
       - Structure: Platform вҶ’ Location вҶ’ Day вҶ’ Artifacts
       - Fields: RECORD_ID, ARTIFACT, STATUS, TIMESTAMP, LAST_MODIFIED
       - Audience: Compliance officers, auditors

     3 Data Sources

     1. PROJECTS - From projects_master table (14 fields)
     2. TENDERS - From tenders table (8 fields)
     3. FINANCIALS - From purchase_orders + invoices (10 fields)

     Features

     - Dynamic Pivoting: Group by Platform, Location, or Day
     - Hierarchical View: Audit profile shows nested tree structure
     - Search: Live filtering via QUERY_ENGINE_CACHE
     - CSV Export: Secure export via safeExportToCSV() (prevents formula
     injection)
     - HTML Export: Print-friendly reports via generateHTMLReport() (not yet
      UI-integrated)

     Export Security

     CVE Prevention: CSV Formula Injection protection
     - Escapes dangerous prefixes: =, +, -, @
     - MCE Compliance v2.0 mandatory requirement
     - Auto-generates timestamped filenames: report_2026-01-29.csv

     ---
     DESIGN STRUCTURE CONCERNS

     1. Component Duplication

     Issue: Multiple components serve similar purposes
     - RiskHeatmap vs RiskHeatmapV2
     - TenderList vs TendersDueSoonPanel
     - NotificationsPanel vs NotificationsPage

     Resolution: Keep V2 versions, archive old ones, update docs

     ---
     2. Dashboard vs Executive Cockpit Overlap

     Confirmed: Both should be kept (dual-dashboard pattern)
     - Dashboard = Operations hub (23 widgets, dense)
     - Executive Cockpit = Leadership overview (3 tabs, minimal)

     Optimization Needed:
     - Extract shared KPI calculation logic into reusable hook
     - Unify risk visualization (use RiskHeatmapV2 in both)
     - Add cross-navigation buttons

     ---
     3. Reports Integration

     Current: Reports is standalone page
     Consideration: Should reports be:
     - вң… Standalone page (current) - Easier to navigate, dedicated
     workspace
     - вқҢ Dashboard widget - Too complex for widget, needs full page
     - вқҢ Executive Cockpit tab - Wrong audience (reports are for ops teams
     too)

     Decision: Keep as standalone page вң…

     ---
     4. Data Hook Architecture

     Current: 10 specialized hooks
     Question: Too fragmented?

     Analysis:
     - useDashboardData - General purpose вң…
     - useReports - Reports-specific вң…
     - useExecutiveData - Executive-specific вң…
     - useDashboardLogic - Business logic separation вң…
     - Others - Feature-specific, appropriate вң…

     Decision: Hook separation is appropriate, aids maintainability вң…

     ---
     DASHBOARD DESIGN ASSESSMENT: 2026 STANDARDS

     User Requirement: "Extremely clean, slick, and most importantly 2026 in
      style"

     Current Status: Mixed - has modern elements but needs refinement

     ---
     CURRENT DASHBOARD ANALYSIS

     What's Working (2026-Aligned) вң…

     1. Glassmorphism & Depth
       - Dark glass panels with backdrop blur
       - Layered surfaces with subtle shadows
       - вң… Modern, on-trend
     2. Information Architecture
       - Clear hierarchy: KPIs вҶ’ Projects вҶ’ Risk
       - Signal-driven alerts at top
       - вң… Good prioritization
     3. Real-time Elements
       - Live sync countdown (T-Minus timer)
       - Pulsing indicators for critical items
       - вң… Dynamic, responsive
     4. Micro-interactions
       - Hover effects with scale transforms
       - Animated progress bars
       - Fade-in transitions
       - вң… Polished feel

     What's Outdated (Not 2026) вқҢ

     1. Visual Overload
       - 23 components = too cluttered
       - "Cyberpunk/industrial" aesthetic feels 2022-2023
       - Neon cyan/teal accents are dated
       - вқҢ Not clean or minimal
     2. Layout Density
       - Too much happening at once
       - No breathing room (gap-6 is tight)
       - Information hierarchy unclear
       - вқҢ Overwhelming, not slick
     3. Color Palette
       - Heavy neon usage (cyan, emerald, rose)
       - High contrast everywhere
       - вқҢ Feels aggressive, not sophisticated
     4. Typography
       - Uppercase tracking-widest everywhere
       - Multiple font sizes without clear system
       - вқҢ Lacks refinement
     5. Missing 2026 Patterns
       - вқҢ No AI copilot integration
       - вқҢ No natural language interface
       - вқҢ No adaptive/contextual layout
       - вқҢ No ambient animations
       - вқҢ No spatial design (depth layers)

     ---
     2026 DESIGN STANDARDS

     Based on current trends (Apple Vision Pro, Linear, Vercel, Arc Browser,
      Notion AI):

     Core Principles

     1. Calm Technology
       - Information appears when needed
       - Ambient awareness, not constant alerts
       - Subtle gradients, not neon
     2. Spatial Design
       - True depth with parallax
       - Frosted glass with depth blur
       - Floating elements
       - Z-axis layering
     3. AI-Native
       - Copilot always accessible
       - Contextual suggestions
       - Natural language queries
       - Predictive UI
     4. Minimal Maximalism
       - Dense information, clean presentation
       - White space is intentional
       - Typography does heavy lifting
       - Color used sparingly
     5. Motion Design
       - Purposeful animations
       - Elastic easing (not linear)
       - State transitions feel physical
       - Hover states are subtle

     ---
     RECOMMENDATIONS: 2026 DASHBOARD REDESIGN

     Option A: Evolution (Keep Structure, Refine Aesthetics) рҹҺЁ

     Effort: 2-3 weeks
     Risk: Low

     Changes:

     1. Color Palette Refinement
     /* Replace neon with sophisticated neutrals */
     --primary: #f5f5f7;      /* Near-white (Apple-grade) */
     --secondary: #1d1d1f;    /* Deep charcoal */
     --accent: #0071e3;       /* Subtle blue (not neon) */
     --success: #30d158;      /* Modern green */
     --warning: #ff9f0a;      /* Warm amber */
     --critical: #ff453a;     /* Refined red */

     /* Glassmorphism */
     --glass: rgba(29, 29, 31, 0.72);
     --glass-border: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08);
     2. Typography System
     /* SF Pro Display / Inter Variable */
     --font-display: 'SF Pro Display', system-ui;
     --font-body: 'Inter Variable', system-ui;

     /* Hierarchy */
     --text-hero: 48px / 1.1 / 600;
     --text-title: 24px / 1.2 / 600;
     --text-body: 16px / 1.5 / 400;
     --text-caption: 13px / 1.4 / 400;

     /* Remove ALL-CAPS tracking-widest */
     3. Spacing System
     /* More generous breathing room */
     --space-xs: 8px;
     --space-sm: 16px;
     --space-md: 24px;   /* Default gap */
     --space-lg: 48px;
     --space-xl: 96px;
     4. Component Consolidation
       - Reduce 23 вҶ’ 12 components
       - Merge duplicates:
           - RiskHeatmap + RiskHeatmapV2 вҶ’ Single version
         - TenderList + TendersDueSoonPanel вҶ’ Unified
       - Archive deprecated: NotificationsPanel, SystemStatusConsole
     5. Layout Simplification
       - Remove Signal Cards at top (too noisy)
       - Make KPI band cleaner (larger numbers, less decoration)
       - Reduce right sticky panel width (400px вҶ’ 320px)
       - Add more white space between sections

     Result: Cleaner, more sophisticated, still recognizable

     FOOTER: Quick Actions (Floating FAB)

     Key Features:

     1. AI Copilot (Persistent)
       - Floating panel (right side, collapsible)
       - Natural language: "Show me projects behind schedule"
       - Proactive suggestions: "3 invoices need approval"
       - Contextual to current view
     2. Adaptive Layout
       - Dashboard changes based on:
           - Time of day
         - User role
         - Recent activity
         - System signals
       - Shows what you need, when you need it
     3. Command Palette (вҢҳK)
       - Universal search
       - Quick actions
       - Navigate anywhere
       - AI-powered suggestions
     4. Minimal Cards
       - Max 3 cards visible at once
       - Large, spacious design
       - Focus on one thing
       - Swipe/pagination for more
     5. Spatial Depth
       - True parallax scrolling
       - Floating elements on hover
       - Depth blur on background
       - Feels 3D

     Design Language:

     /* Apple Vision Pro inspired */
     --surface: rgba(18, 18, 18, 0.7);
     --surface-elevated: rgba(28, 28, 30, 0.85);
     --blur: blur(40px) saturate(180%);

     /* Soft shadows */
     --shadow-soft: 0 8px 32px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12);
     --shadow-lifted: 0 20px 60px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.24);

     /* Elastic animations */
     --ease-elastic: cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55);
     --ease-smooth: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);

     Result: Cutting-edge, AI-first, truly 2026

       50% { opacity: 1; }

     Current Issues:
     - ALL CAPS everywhere (looks aggressive)
     - tracking-widest (hard to read)
     - Inconsistent sizing

     2026 Standard:

     /* Hierarchy */
     h1 { font: 600 48px/1.1 'SF Pro Display'; }
     h2 { font: 600 32px/1.2 'SF Pro Display'; }
     h3 { font: 600 24px/1.3 'SF Pro Display'; }
     body { font: 400 16px/1.5 'Inter Variable'; }
     caption { font: 400 13px/1.4 'Inter Variable'; color:
     rgba(255,255,255,0.6); }

     /* NO uppercase unless absolutely necessary */
     /* Use sentence case for everything */

     ---
     INFRASTRUCTURE UPDATES (2026-01-29)

     Changes Made During Rate Limit:

     1. вң… Clerk Middleware Fixed (middleware.ts)

     Previous Issue: Middleware was bypassed completely, causing auth 
     warnings.

     Solution Applied:
     // Conditional middleware based on env var
     const clerkEnabled =
     Boolean((process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY ?? '').trim());

     const middleware = clerkEnabled
       ? clerkMiddleware(async (auth, req) => {
           if (!isPublicRoute(req)) {
             await auth.protect();
           }
         })
       : () => NextResponse.next();

     Impact:
     - вң… Proper Clerk authentication when enabled
     - вң… Graceful fallback when disabled (demo mode)
     - вң… Public routes for AI health endpoints: /api/ai/ready,
     /api/ai/health, /api/ai/version
     - вң… Resolves auth() warnings from earlier diagnostic runs

     Status: PRODUCTION-READY вң…

     ---
     2. вң… RAG Bulk Ingestion Disabled (app/api/rag/ingest-all/route.ts)

     Previous Issue: Bulk ingestion could timeout on Vercel (5-minute
     limit).

     Solution Applied:
     // Returns 410 (Gone) status
     return NextResponse.json({
       outcome: 'failed',
       error: {
         code: 'LEGACY_ENDPOINT_DISABLED',
         message: 'Bulk RAG ingestion is disabled on Vercel. Use the 
     external AI Gateway indexing API/worker.'
       }
     }, { status: 410 });

     Impact:
     - вң… Prevents timeout errors in production
     - вң… Clear error message directs users to external worker
     - вң… Vercel-optimized architecture
     - вң… Individual ingestion still works via /api/rag/ingest

     Status: PRODUCTION-OPTIMIZED вң…

     ---
     PRODUCTION ARCHITECTURE: AI GATEWAY + VERCEL

     Critical Discovery: AI agents require VM-hosted AI Gateway to function.

     System Architecture

     в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
     в”Ӯ TIER 1: FRONTEND (Vercel / Next.js)                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - UI components (Dashboard, AgentConsole, etc.)          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Thin API proxy routes (/api/ai/*)                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Proxies requests to AI Gateway via AI_GATEWAY_URL      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - NO direct Gemini calls, NO RAG processing              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Bot status: Mirrors AI Gateway /readyz via /api/ai/readyв”Ӯ
     в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
                                 вҶ“ HTTPS
     в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
     в”Ӯ TIER 2: AI GATEWAY (GCP VM, Docker Container)              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Docker image: nexus-ai-gateway                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Framework: FastAPI (Python)                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Runs on VM at localhost:8000                            в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Exposed publicly via HTTPS (Caddy/Nginx reverse proxy) в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   Endpoints:                                                в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     GET  /health    вҶ’ Process up check                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     POST /chat      вҶ’ RAG + Gemini response                 в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     GET  /readyz    вҶ’ Full readiness check (future)         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     GET  /version   вҶ’ AI Gateway version                    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     GET  /metrics   вҶ’ Prometheus metrics (future)           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   Environment (.env in ai_service/):                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - SUPABASE_URL                                          в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY (Service Role)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - GEMINI_API_KEY                                        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   Capabilities:                                             в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - Hybrid RAG retrieval (Supabase RPC)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - Gemini API calls                                      в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - Document embedding generation                         в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ     - Vector similarity search                              в”Ӯ
     в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
                                 вҶ“ PostgreSQL
     в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
     в”Ӯ TIER 3: DATA PLANE (Supabase PostgreSQL)                   в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - System-of-record for ERP data                           в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - document_embeddings table (vector storage)              в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - RPC: match_documents_hybrid (retrieval function)        в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ   - Ingestion: manual_ingest.py (populates embeddings)      в”Ӯ
     в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

     Network Security (VM)

     Recommended Setup:
     Public Internet (HTTPS:443)
         вҶ“
